	$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/OIDplusPagePublicWhois.css');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/OIDplusPagePublicWhois.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/publicPages/100_whois/OIDplusPagePublicWhois.css', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
